PINgrid produces a one-time code (OTC) to prove who you are and all you have to remember is a simple pattern, no PINs or passwords. PINgrid keeps your pattern a secret by never revealing it when you log on. Each time you log in you enter a new code however your pattern remains the same and is secret to you.\r\n\r\nWhilst PINgrid can be used as a traditional 2 Factor Authentication solution it also suits many other scenarios.
